
============== high level task decomposition ================
[{'objective': 'Determine the least prime number p for which there exists a positive integer n such that p² divides n⁴ + 1'}, {'objective': 'Find the least positive integer n such that n⁴ + 1 is divisible by p²'}]
============== task analysis ================
1. Extract and Summarize Given Information:
- There is a prime number p, defined as the least prime for which there exists a positive integer n such that p^2 divides n^4 + 1.
- The problem involves the expression n^4 + 1, a quartic polynomial evaluated at integer values.
- The divisibility condition is that p^2 | n^4 + 1, meaning n^4 + 1 is divisible by the square of the prime p.
- After identifying such a prime p, the problem asks for the least positive integer m such that m^4 + 1 is divisible by p^2.

2. Analyze Relationships Between Components:
- The key relationship is the divisibility of n^4 + 1 by p^2, which implies that n^4 ≡ -1 (mod p^2).
- Since p is prime, the problem involves modular arithmetic and properties of residues modulo prime powers.
- The condition that p^2 divides n^4 + 1 is stronger than just p dividing n^4 + 1; it requires a higher-order congruence.
- The minimality of p suggests that smaller primes do not satisfy this condition for any positive integer n.
- The problem implicitly involves the multiplicative order of n modulo p^2 and the structure of the group of units modulo p^2.
- Finding the least m with the same divisibility condition relates to finding the smallest solution to the congruence m^4 ≡ -1 (mod p^2).

3. Identify the Field of Study:
- The problem lies primarily in number theory.
- Subfields involved include modular arithmetic, prime number theory, and possibly algebraic number theory (due to the quartic expression and divisibility by prime squares).
- Concepts such as orders modulo prime powers, lifting solutions from modulo p to modulo p^2 (Hensel's lemma), and properties of quartic residues are relevant.
- Such problems commonly appear in mathematical competitions and research in number theory.

4. Highlight Aspects Needing Clarification:
- The problem does not specify whether n and m must be positive integers only, but it is implied.
- It is not explicitly stated whether multiple n or m exist; the problem focuses on the least prime p and least positive integer m.
- The problem assumes familiarity with divisibility by prime squares and modular arithmetic at higher powers.
- Potential challenges include determining the existence of solutions modulo p^2 and ensuring minimality conditions.
- The problem does not provide explicit bounds or ranges for n or m, which may affect computational approaches.

async def forward(self, taskInfo):
    from collections import Counter
    print("Task Requirement: ", taskInfo)
    sub_tasks = []
    agents = []
    logs = []

    cot_instruction_1 = "Sub-task 1: Analyze the divisibility condition n^4 + 1 ≡ 0 (mod p) for prime p and determine necessary conditions on p for the existence of n satisfying this congruence. Emphasize the implications for p dividing n^4 + 1 and the nature of quartic residues modulo p. Avoid attempting to solve modulo p^2 at this stage."
    cot_agent_1 = LLMAgentBase(["thinking", "answer"], "Chain-of-Thought Agent", model=self.node_model, temperature=0.0)
    subtask_desc1 = {
        "subtask_id": "subtask_1",
        "instruction": cot_instruction_1,
        "context": ["user query"],
        "agent_collaboration": "CoT"
    }
    thinking1, answer1 = await cot_agent_1([taskInfo], cot_instruction_1, is_sub_task=True)
    agents.append(f"CoT agent {cot_agent_1.id}, analyzing divisibility modulo p, thinking: {thinking1.content}; answer: {answer1.content}")
    sub_tasks.append(f"Sub-task 1 output: thinking - {thinking1.content}; answer - {answer1.content}")
    subtask_desc1['response'] = {
        "thinking": thinking1,
        "answer": answer1
    }
    logs.append(subtask_desc1)
    print("Step 1: ", sub_tasks[-1])

    cot_sc_instruction_2 = "Sub-task 2: Based on the output from Sub-task 1, determine the conditions under which the congruence n^4 + 1 ≡ 0 (mod p^2) can be lifted from solutions modulo p to modulo p^2, using tools such as Hensel's lemma or equivalent lifting criteria. Focus on the existence of solutions modulo p^2 given solutions modulo p, without yet identifying specific primes or integers."
    N_sc = self.max_sc
    cot_agents_2 = [LLMAgentBase(["thinking", "answer"], "Chain-of-Thought Agent", model=self.node_model, temperature=0.0) for _ in range(N_sc)]
    possible_answers_2 = []
    possible_thinkings_2 = []
    subtask_desc2 = {
        "subtask_id": "subtask_2",
        "instruction": cot_sc_instruction_2,
        "context": ["user query", "thinking of subtask 1"],
        "agent_collaboration": "SC_CoT"
    }
    for i in range(N_sc):
        thinking2, answer2 = await cot_agents_2[i]([taskInfo, thinking1], cot_sc_instruction_2, is_sub_task=True)
        agents.append(f"CoT-SC agent {cot_agents_2[i].id}, determining lifting conditions, thinking: {thinking2.content}; answer: {answer2.content}")
        possible_answers_2.append(answer2)
        possible_thinkings_2.append(thinking2)
    final_decision_agent_2 = LLMAgentBase(["thinking", "answer"], "Final Decision Agent", model=self.node_model, temperature=0.0)
    final_instr_2 = "Given all the above thinking and answers, find the most consistent and correct solutions for the lifting conditions of the congruence modulo p^2."
    thinking2, answer2 = await final_decision_agent_2([taskInfo] + possible_thinkings_2, "Sub-task 2: Determine lifting conditions." + final_instr_2, is_sub_task=True)
    sub_tasks.append(f"Sub-task 2 output: thinking - {thinking2.content}; answer - {answer2.content}")
    subtask_desc2['response'] = {
        "thinking": thinking2,
        "answer": answer2
    }
    logs.append(subtask_desc2)
    print("Step 2: ", sub_tasks[-1])

    debate_instr_3 = "Sub-task 3: Identify the smallest prime p for which there exists a positive integer n such that p^2 divides n^4 + 1, by combining the results from subtasks 1 and 2. This involves checking primes in ascending order and verifying the lifting condition for each. Avoid exhaustive search without theoretical pruning. Given solutions to the problem from other agents, consider their opinions as additional advice. Please think carefully and provide an updated answer."
    debate_agents_3 = [LLMAgentBase(["thinking", "answer"], "Debate Agent", model=self.node_model, role=role, temperature=0.0) for role in self.debate_role]
    N_max_3 = self.max_round
    all_thinking3 = [[] for _ in range(N_max_3)]
    all_answer3 = [[] for _ in range(N_max_3)]
    subtask_desc3 = {
        "subtask_id": "subtask_3",
        "instruction": debate_instr_3,
        "context": ["user query", "thinking of subtask 1", "thinking of subtask 2"],
        "agent_collaboration": "Debate"
    }
    for r in range(N_max_3):
        for i, agent in enumerate(debate_agents_3):
            if r == 0:
                thinking3, answer3 = await agent([taskInfo, thinking1, thinking2], debate_instr_3, r, is_sub_task=True)
            else:
                input_infos_3 = [taskInfo, thinking1, thinking2] + all_thinking3[r-1]
                thinking3, answer3 = await agent(input_infos_3, debate_instr_3, r, is_sub_task=True)
            agents.append(f"Debate agent {agent.id}, round {r}, identifying smallest prime p, thinking: {thinking3.content}; answer: {answer3.content}")
            all_thinking3[r].append(thinking3)
            all_answer3[r].append(answer3)
    final_decision_agent_3 = LLMAgentBase(["thinking", "answer"], "Final Decision Agent", model=self.node_model, temperature=0.0)
    final_instr_3 = "Given all the above thinking and answers, reason over them carefully and provide a final answer for the smallest prime p."
    thinking3, answer3 = await final_decision_agent_3([taskInfo] + all_thinking3[-1], "Sub-task 3: Identify smallest prime p." + final_instr_3, is_sub_task=True)
    sub_tasks.append(f"Sub-task 3 output: thinking - {thinking3.content}; answer - {answer3.content}")
    subtask_desc3['response'] = {
        "thinking": thinking3,
        "answer": answer3
    }
    logs.append(subtask_desc3)
    print("Step 3: ", sub_tasks[-1])

    cot_sc_instruction_4 = "Sub-task 4: For the identified prime p, find the least positive integer m such that m^4 + 1 is divisible by p^2. This requires solving the congruence m^4 ≡ -1 (mod p^2) and selecting the minimal positive solution. Avoid considering values not congruent modulo p^2 or ignoring minimality."
    N_sc_4 = self.max_sc
    cot_agents_4 = [LLMAgentBase(["thinking", "answer"], "Chain-of-Thought Agent", model=self.node_model, temperature=0.0) for _ in range(N_sc_4)]
    possible_answers_4 = []
    possible_thinkings_4 = []
    subtask_desc4 = {
        "subtask_id": "subtask_4",
        "instruction": cot_sc_instruction_4,
        "context": ["user query", "thinking of subtask 3"],
        "agent_collaboration": "SC_CoT"
    }
    for i in range(N_sc_4):
        thinking4, answer4 = await cot_agents_4[i]([taskInfo, thinking3], cot_sc_instruction_4, is_sub_task=True)
        agents.append(f"CoT-SC agent {cot_agents_4[i].id}, finding least positive integer m, thinking: {thinking4.content}; answer: {answer4.content}")
        possible_answers_4.append(answer4)
        possible_thinkings_4.append(thinking4)
    final_decision_agent_4 = LLMAgentBase(["thinking", "answer"], "Final Decision Agent", model=self.node_model, temperature=0.0)
    final_instr_4 = "Given all the above thinking and answers, find the most consistent and correct least positive integer m satisfying the divisibility condition."
    thinking4, answer4 = await final_decision_agent_4([taskInfo] + possible_thinkings_4, "Sub-task 4: Find least positive integer m." + final_instr_4, is_sub_task=True)
    sub_tasks.append(f"Sub-task 4 output: thinking - {thinking4.content}; answer - {answer4.content}")
    subtask_desc4['response'] = {
        "thinking": thinking4,
        "answer": answer4
    }
    logs.append(subtask_desc4)
    print("Step 4: ", sub_tasks[-1])

    reflect_inst_5 = "Given previous attempts and feedback, carefully consider where you could go wrong in your latest attempt. Using insights from previous attempts, try to solve the task better."
    cot_reflect_instruction_5 = "Sub-task 5: Verify and validate the solution m found in subtask 4 by explicitly checking the divisibility condition m^4 + 1 ≡ 0 (mod p^2). Confirm minimality and correctness of m, ensuring no smaller positive integer satisfies the condition. Avoid assumptions without verification." + reflect_inst_5
    cot_agent_5 = LLMAgentBase(["thinking", "answer"], "Chain-of-Thought Agent", model=self.node_model, temperature=0.0)
    critic_agent_5 = LLMAgentBase(["feedback", "correct"], "Critic Agent", model=self.node_model, temperature=0.0)
    N_max_5 = self.max_round
    cot_inputs_5 = [taskInfo, thinking4, answer4]
    subtask_desc5 = {
        "subtask_id": "subtask_5",
        "instruction": cot_reflect_instruction_5,
        "context": ["user query", "thinking of subtask 4"],
        "agent_collaboration": "Reflexion"
    }
    thinking5, answer5 = await cot_agent_5(cot_inputs_5, cot_reflect_instruction_5, 0, is_sub_task=True)
    agents.append(f"Reflexion CoT agent {cot_agent_5.id}, verifying solution m, thinking: {thinking5.content}; answer: {answer5.content}")
    critic_inst_5 = "Please review the answer above and criticize on where might be wrong. If you are absolutely sure it is correct, output exactly 'True' in 'correct'"
    for i in range(N_max_5):
        feedback, correct = await critic_agent_5([taskInfo, thinking5], "Please review and provide the limitations of provided solutions." + critic_inst_5, i, is_sub_task=True)
        agents.append(f"Critic agent {critic_agent_5.id}, providing feedback, thinking: {feedback.content}; answer: {correct.content}")
        if correct.content == "True":
            break
        cot_inputs_5.extend([thinking5, feedback])
        thinking5, answer5 = await cot_agent_5(cot_inputs_5, cot_reflect_instruction_5, i + 1, is_sub_task=True)
        agents.append(f"Reflexion CoT agent {cot_agent_5.id}, refining verification, thinking: {thinking5.content}; answer: {answer5.content}")
    sub_tasks.append(f"Sub-task 5 output: thinking - {thinking5.content}; answer - {answer5.content}")
    subtask_desc5['response'] = {
        "thinking": thinking5,
        "answer": answer5
    }
    logs.append(subtask_desc5)
    print("Step 5: ", sub_tasks[-1])

    final_answer = await self.make_final_answer(thinking5, answer5, sub_tasks, agents)
    return final_answer, logs

async def forward(self, taskInfo):
    from collections import Counter
    print("Task Requirement: ", taskInfo)
    sub_tasks = []
    agents = []
    logs = []

    # Stage 1: Analyze divisibility conditions modulo p and lifting to p^2

    # Sub-task 1: Analyze n^4 + 1 ≡ 0 (mod p) with Debate
    debate_instr_1 = (
        "Sub-task 1: Analyze the divisibility condition n^4 + 1 ≡ 0 (mod p) for a prime p. "
        "Determine necessary and sufficient conditions on p for the existence of a positive integer n satisfying this congruence. "
        "Focus on quartic residues modulo p and implications for p dividing n^4 + 1. "
        "Avoid attempting to solve modulo p^2 at this stage and do not assume existence of solutions without proof. "
        "Given solutions to the problem from other agents, consider their opinions as additional advice. Please think carefully and provide an updated answer."
    )
    debate_agents_1 = [LLMAgentBase(["thinking", "answer"], "Debate Agent", model=self.node_model, role=role, temperature=0.0) for role in self.debate_role]
    N_max_1 = self.max_round
    all_thinking_1 = [[] for _ in range(N_max_1)]
    all_answer_1 = [[] for _ in range(N_max_1)]
    subtask_desc1 = {
        "subtask_id": "subtask_1",
        "instruction": debate_instr_1,
        "context": ["user query"],
        "agent_collaboration": "Debate"
    }
    for r in range(N_max_1):
        for i, agent in enumerate(debate_agents_1):
            if r == 0:
                thinking1, answer1 = await agent([taskInfo], debate_instr_1, r, is_sub_task=True)
            else:
                input_infos_1 = [taskInfo] + all_thinking_1[r-1]
                thinking1, answer1 = await agent(input_infos_1, debate_instr_1, r, is_sub_task=True)
            agents.append(f"Debate agent {agent.id}, round {r}, analyzing divisibility mod p, thinking: {thinking1.content}; answer: {answer1.content}")
            all_thinking_1[r].append(thinking1)
            all_answer_1[r].append(answer1)
    final_decision_agent_1 = LLMAgentBase(["thinking", "answer"], "Final Decision Agent", model=self.node_model, temperature=0.0)
    final_instr_1 = "Sub-task 1: Given all the above thinking and answers, reason over them carefully and provide a final answer."
    thinking1, answer1 = await final_decision_agent_1([taskInfo] + all_thinking_1[-1], final_instr_1, is_sub_task=True)
    agents.append(f"Final Decision agent, Sub-task 1, thinking: {thinking1.content}; answer: {answer1.content}")
    sub_tasks.append(f"Sub-task 1 output: thinking - {thinking1.content}; answer - {answer1.content}")

Also, n cannot be congruent to 0 modulo p because then n^4 + 1 ≡ 1 (mod p), not 0. Therefore, f'(n) = 4n^3 ≠ 0 (mod p). This satisfies the condition of Hensel's lemma, guaranteeing a unique lift of the solution modulo p to modulo p^2. Hence, any solution modulo p to n^4 + 1 ≡ 0 (mod p) can be uniquely lifted to a solution modulo p^2. The limitation is the prime p=2, which does not satisfy the problem's conditions, and the fact that lifting solutions modulo p to modulo p^2 does not guarantee the existence of an integer n such that p^2 divides n^4 + 1, only that solutions modulo p^2 exist. In summary, the most consistent and correct lifting condition is that the derivative f'(n) = 4n^3 is not congruent to zero modulo p at the solution n, which holds for all solutions modulo p for primes p > 2, ensuring the applicability of Hensel's lemma and unique lifting to modulo p^2."], 'agent_collaboration': 'Debate', 'response': {'thinking': Info(name='thinking', author='Final Decision Agent azyw', content="The problem requires identifying candidate primes p for which there exists a positive integer n such that p^2 divides n^4 + 1.
